 surya grahan ke bare main kaha jaataa he ki iskaa asar hamaare grahon kii sthiti ko prabhavit karata he

 kya he 'surya grahan'?surya kii parikrama prithvi karti he or chandramaa prithvi kii parikrama karata he
 They keep coming in between each other during the parikrama
 jab surya or prithvi ke bich chandramaa aa jaae to ise surya grahan kehete hai
 It affects the Earth and the people of Earth
 surya grahan kya hota he or ye khagoleey ghatana kaise hoti he ye to hamane aapako bataa diya, lekin ab aapako bataate hai ki is baar ke surya grahan main khaas kya he

 - This solar eclipse is partially visible in India
 - bharat main surya grahan kii kul avadhi 30 minute he or grahan kumbh raashi main lag rahaa he
 General Effect of Solar Eclipse- In this eclipse, Ketu is being formed by association of Ketu
 is grahan main chandramaa, shukr, budh kaa yoga bhi he
 - Due to the influence of Sun and Ketu, chances of accidents are being created
 - raajnneetik rup se bhayankar uthal-puthal much sakati he
 Jupiter also has an eye, so taking measures will benefit
 -jin sthanon par grahan dikh rahaa haivehaan sutak ke niyam lagu hai
 Effect of 'solar eclipse' You came to know about the effects of solar eclipse but now the question arises whether solar eclipse is really a bad event
 
 
 
 - Solar eclipse is an astronomical event
 - iskaa asar man par jarur padataa he
 - It is not necessary that the impact of the eclipse is bad, in the eclipse, the sky is in a wonderful state
